)@@G@@  . USERS REL PKT ADR               . SDGET     *[S@@@*SDFF*@A@@@]      PJ
)@@G@@   THE @SORTSDF PROCESSOR     @^@@@]4GENERAL DESCRIPTION    @G@@@] THE @PK
)@@G@@SORTSDF PROCESSOR READS AN SDF FILE AND PRODUCES A NEW SDF FILE   @G@@@]PL
)@@G@@ SORTED ALPHANUMERICALLY ACCORDING TO THE KEY FIELDS SPECIFIED ON THE   PM
)@@G@@@E@@@] PROCESSOR CALL CARD.  UP TO 15 KEY FIELDS ARE ALLOWED.     @F@@@]PN
)@@G@@ THE INPUT AND OUTPUT FILES MAY EXIST EITHER ON MASS-STORAGE OR   @F@@@]PO
)@@G@@ MAGNETIC TAPE.  IF THE OUTPUT FILE IS MAGNETIC TAPE, IT WILL BE  @G@@@]PP
)@@G@@ REWOUND BEFORE AND AFTER IT IS WRITTEN.  THE OUTPUT FILE MAY ALSO BE   PQ
)@@G@@@ @@@] THE SAME AS THE INPUT FILE.  @]@@@]SPACE 3     @G@@@]  SDF FILES PR
)@@G@@ARE CREATED BY THE @DATA PROCESSOR AND THE @ED PROCESSOR.   @F@@@] ALTERPS
)@@G@@NATE CARD-PUNCH FILES CREATED BY COBOL AND FILES CREATED BY @G@@@] FORTRPT
)@@G@@AN FORMATTED WRITE STATEMENTS ARE ALSO IN SDF FORMAT AND MAY BE   @A@@@]PU
)@@G@@ SORTED WITH THE @SORTSDF PROCESSOR.@]@@@]SPACE 2     @G@@@] NOTE:  FORTPV
)@@G@@RAN CARRIAGE CONTROL RECORDS ARE LOST ALONG WITH BACKWARD   @G@@@] LINKSPW
)@@G@@ SO A FORTRAN BACKSPACE STATEMENT SHOULD NOT REFERENCE A FILE     @B@@@]PX
)@@G@@ THAT HAS BE PROCESSED WITH @SORTSDF.     @#@@@]4TECHNICAL DETAILS@G@@@]PY
)@@G@@ @SORTSDF USES THE STANDARD UNIVAC SORT PACKAGE AND THE SYSTEM ROUTINES PZ
)@@G@@@F@@@] SDFI AND SDFO TO READ AND WRITE SDF FILES. THE MASS-STORAGE FILESQA
)@@G@@@H@@@] (XA AND XB) AND CORE (R$CORE) NEEDED BY THE SORT PACKAGE ARE DYNAQB
)@@G@@MICALLY     @D@@@] ASSIGNED AND RELEASED BY THE @SORTSDF PROCESSOR.     QC
)@@G@@@]@@@]SPACE 2     @E@@@] * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * *QD
)@@G@@ * * * *    @^@@@] IMPLEMENTATION NOTE:   @C@@@] MASS-STORAGE FILE XB ISQE
)@@G@@ DYNAMICALLY ASSIGNED TO@D@@@] FASTRAND DRUM WITH A DEVICE TYPE OF F2.  QF
)@@G@@IF YOUR     @C@@@] INSTALLATION HAS NO FASTRAND DRUMS OR LOTS OF  @B@@@]QG
)@@G@@ HIGH-SPEED DRUMS (F4,F17) THE F2 SHOULD  @E@@@] BE CHANGED ACCORDINGLY QH
)@@G@@ON CARD 9 IN DECK SORTF/SORTSDF.    @E@@@] * * * * * * * * * * * * * * *QI
)@@G@@ * * * * * * * * * * * * *    @^@@@]4PROCESSOR CALL CARD    @F@@@] ASSUMQJ
)@@G@@ING THE @SORTSDF PROCESSOR EXISTS IN THE THE SYSTEM LIBRARY @C@@@] (SYS$QK
)@@G@@*LIB$.) OR IN TPF$, THE PROCESSOR CALL IS:@]@@@]SPACE 3     @F@#@]  @SORQL
)@@G@@TSDF INPUT.,OUTPUT.,NREC,RSIZE,KEY/SCHAR/NCHAR.ORDER,...    @F@@@# @SORTQM
)@@G@@SDF,OPTIONS IN.,OUT.,NREC,RSIZE,KEY/SCHAR/NCHAR.ORDER,..    @]@@@]SPACE QN
)@@G@@2     @]@@@] WHERE:     @C@#@]         INPUT   - IS THE NAME OF THE INPUQO
)@@G@@T FILE@C@@@#         IN      - IS THE NAME OF THE INPUT FILE@D@#@]      QP
)@@G@@   OUTPUT  - IS THE NAME OF THE OUTPUT FILE     @D@@@#         OUT     -QQ
)@@G@@ IS THE NAME OF THE OUTPUT FILE     @E@@@]         NREC    - INTEGER GIVQR
)@@G@@ING THE APPROXIMATE NUMBER    @C@@@]                   OF RECORDS IN THEQS
)@@G@@ INPUT FILE @D@@@]         RSIZE   - INTEGER GIVING SIZE OF INPUT RECORDQT
)@@G@@@A@@@]                   IN CHARACTERS    @F@@@]         KEY     - IS THQU
)@@G@@E CHARACTERS 'KEY' INDICATING A KEY FIELD @ @@@]                   DESCRQV
)@@G@@IPTOR @F@@@]         SCHAR   - INTEGER GIVING THE LEFTMOST CHARACTER POSQW
)@@G@@ITION @D@@@]                   OF THIS KEY FIELD WITHIN THE RECORD@D@@@]QX
)@@G@@                   ( CHARACTERS NUMBERED LEFT TO RIGHT@A@@@]            QY
)@@G@@       STARTING AT 1 )  @G@@@]         NCHAR   - INTEGER GIVING NUMBER OQZ
)@@G@@F CHARACTERS IN KEY FIELD     @E@@@]         ORDER   - CHARACTER 'A' FORRA
)@@G@@ ASCENDING  SORT OR     @D@@@]                   CHARACTER 'D' FOR DESCERB
)@@G@@NDING SORT  @]@@@#SPACE 2     @]@#@]SPACE 2     @ @@@#  ALLOWABLE OPTIONRC
)@@G@@S ARE :     @F@@@#          'A' - INPUT FILE IS ASCII.  THE OUTPUT FILE RD
)@@G@@WILL BE     @ @@@#                THE SAME.     @E@@@#          'L' - LIRE
)@@G@@ST THE SORTED OUTPUT FILE AS IT IS WRITTEN@E@@@#          'M' - MERGE CARF
)@@G@@RDS READ FROM THE RUNSTREAM INTO THE@F@@@#                OUTPUT FILE.  RG
)@@G@@IF THE INPUT FILE FIELD IS NULL,    @E@@@#                THE OUTPUT FILRH
)@@G@@E WILL CONSIST ENTIRELY OF    @E@@@#                THE CARDS READ FROM RI
)@@G@@THE RUNSTREAM.  IF THE  @E@^@#                 INPUT FILE FIELD IS NULL,RJ
)@@G@@ THE OUTPUT FILE  @E@@@^                INPUT FILE FIELD IS NULL, THE OURK
)@@G@@TPUT FILE   @D@^@#                 FIELD MUST BE PRECEDED BY A COMMA.   RL
)@@G@@@D@@@^                FIELD MUST BE PRECEDED BY A COMMA.    @F@@@#      RM
)@@G@@    'D' - USED WITH THE 'M' OPTION TO DELETE ANY RECORDS    @E@@@#      RN
)@@G@@          IN THE INPUT FILE THAT HAVE IDENTICAL KEYS  @D@^@#            RO
)@@G@@     WITH RECORDS READ FROM THE RUNSTREAM.@D@@@^                WITH RECRP
)@@G@@ORDS READ FROM THE RUNSTREAM. @]@@@#SPACE 2     @H@#@] THE KEY FIELD DESRQ
)@@G@@CRIPTOR MAY BE SPECIFIED UP TO 15 TIMES, MAJOR TO MINOR.    @H@@@# THE KRR
)@@G@@EY FIELD DESCRIPTOR MAY BE SPECIFIED UP TO 20 TIMES, MAJOR TO MINOR.    RS
)@@G@@@]@@@]SPACE 2     @E@@@] THE PROCESSOR CALL CARD CAN BE CONTINUED LIKE ART
)@@G@@NY OTHER    @E@@@] EXEC8 CONTROL CARD BY PLACING A ; AFTER A , ON THE FIRU
)@@G@@RST   @E@@@] CARD AND STARTING THE NEXT KEY DESCRIPTOR ON THE FOLLOWING RV
)@@G@@@[@@@] CARD.@]@@@]SPACE 2     @]@@@] EXAMPLE:   @]@@@]SPACE 2     @F@@@]RW
)@@G@@         @SORTSDF  INPUTFILE.,OUTPUTFILE.,3500,80,KEY/4/6.A,;     @ @@@]RX
)@@G@@         KEY/30/2.A,KEY/72/8.D@]@@@]SPACE 2     @#@@@]4SAMPLE USAGE     RY
)@@G@@@G@@@] THE EXAMPLE BELOW SORTS THE CARD IMAGES  IN 'AFILE' FIRST IN ASCERZ
)@@G@@NDING @F@@@] ORDER IN COLUMNS 5-15 AND THEN IN  DESCENDING ORDER IN COLUSA
)@@G@@MNS   @E@@@] 30 TO 32. ( FILE 'AFILE' CONTAINS ABOUT 1000 RECORDS ).    SB
)@@G@@@]@@@]SPACE 5     @ @@@]         @ASG,T   AFILE.,F    @^@@@]         @ASSC
)@@G@@G,T BFILE.,F@^@@@]         @DATA,IL AFILE.@]@@@]         .  @A@@@]      SD
)@@G@@   .    ( CARDS TO BE SORTED )@]@@@]         .  @#@@@]         @END     SE
)@@G@@@F@@@]         @SORTSDF AFILE.,BFILE.,1000,80,KEY/5/10.A,KEY/30/32.D    SF
)@@G@@@A@@@]         @HDG LISTING OF SORTED DATA@^@@@]         @DATA,L BFILE. SG
